function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

}

	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '5b25fd63d14d8ae03ee87085f9c63c87161a318c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '5b25fd63d14d8ae03ee87085f9c63c87161a318c') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'ddf3f88d69e28dca15aaf85d24c6995c3eb29277') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '5b25fd63d14d8ae03ee87085f9c63c87161a318c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('action.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: action.php');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('action.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): action.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('action.php') != 'a08601f8f9e64c53bfbc60ed2f440d508150515c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): action.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('action.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of action.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('action.php') !== 'a08601f8f9e64c53bfbc60ed2f440d508150515c') {
		if (@sha1_file('action.php') !== '5c6df6c3ad96ae909da33b2da1f0a3f3f2896be7') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: action.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('action.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('action.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('action.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('action.php') !== 'a08601f8f9e64c53bfbc60ed2f440d508150515c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): action.php');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') != '2bc42f610f8b658ec8b90cf2580e08d0a0c8e579') {

	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', 0644)) {

	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== '2bc42f610f8b658ec8b90cf2580e08d0a0c8e579') {

			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php') != 'f7ec130f16c5498ce8c41131e669487b1ed43c04') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php') !== 'f7ec130f16c5498ce8c41131e669487b1ed43c04') {

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusTree.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();

if (!is_file('index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index.php');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index.php') != '8dce316c17601d022047f5fa13e0c80c9067e86e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '8dce316c17601d022047f5fa13e0c80c9067e86e') {
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'cacf1c33f3a109ae44839e5f756d372422fef700') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '8dce316c17601d022047f5fa13e0c80c9067e86e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('oidplus.css')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus.css');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('oidplus.css')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus.css');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.css') != '0f55c22689416257405f8e1aa4c3be629706c92c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.css');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.css', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus.css');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.css') !== '0f55c22689416257405f8e1aa4c3be629706c92c') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.css') !== 'dd402213e08d384fe3c3f7762e66fad1057b9c08') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus.css');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus.css');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.css', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.css') !== '0f55c22689416257405f8e1aa4c3be629706c92c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.css');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus.js');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('oidplus.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.js') != '1bf7fc9785fbd6464d97749b245fc952b40070dc') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.js') !== '1bf7fc9785fbd6464d97749b245fc952b40070dc') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.js') !== '5a1e3ad9cf97ba2a2583aac335893b6d77109683') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.js') !== '1bf7fc9785fbd6464d97749b245fc952b40070dc') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.js');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/setup.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/setup.js');
	writefile_13();
	if (!is_file('setup/setup.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/setup.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/setup.js') != '5182ca1b52006556f580d7e99876f469bd374cc3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/setup.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/setup.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/setup.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.js') !== '5182ca1b52006556f580d7e99876f469bd374cc3') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.js') !== '1864f47f1d31f4387f643ff7827849d66b54bf09') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/setup.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/setup.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/setup.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/setup.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_13();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.js') !== '5182ca1b52006556f580d7e99876f469bd374cc3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/setup.js');
		}
	}
}
